# <a name="analytic-trace-event-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="b392e-102">Çözümleme İzleme Etkinliği Başvurusu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b392e-102">Analytic Trace Event Reference</span></span>
